< review>
WARNING TO ALL INCOMING PATIENTS FROM THE IMPERIAL VALLEY!

While all the staff are incredibly kind and hardworking, the Administration WILL NOT PROVIDE TRANSPORTATION FOR DISCHARGE PATIENTS. My father had become bed ridden from his dementia and thus could not walk on his own. Administration argued with my mother on how Hospice should be the one the to provide transportation back to the Imperial Valley or we should pay out of pocket ($500 dollars) when since day one they told us Victoria Post would be able to provide it. We ended up bargaining with them them giving us a wheelchair to compromise because at that time we just wanted to get my father home.

The facility staff on hand were a gift. Everyone there was always great help. Always asking if we were comfortable and my father was taken care of. My 79 year old father had a heart attack that required bypass surgery. After he was released from the hospital he was too weak to return home so the cardiologist recommended a rehab facility to work on his strength. Within five days of physical and occupational therapy he was ready to return home. The staff was great and treated him with respect and provided the care he needed to return to his active life. The rehab staff are all licensed and know their stuff. My father doesn't listen very well and they all took the extra time to make sure he was doing things safe and the proper way. <userid>118030271021262977984</userid><Name>Marvin Garcia< /Name><date>1509214287930<//date>< Rate>
4< /Rate>
< review>
4-Stars = Very Good!  A small, efficient, clean, and bright specialty/eclectic cafe.  Good, attentive service, nice dining atmosphere, compliments a diverse, unique menu.  Also, from the time of the order until we had food on the table...QUICK!!!  I went with my wife, along with dear friends that live in the same city as the cafe.

I had a red velvet waffle that came with a soft cream cheese dollop, enough to cover the whole waffle, and a circle of whipped cream around the waffle's edge. It wasn't crispy like waffles should be.  If you want soft...pancakes!  The waffle itself was 2-star fair, but the dollop of soft cream cheese made the whole mouthful 3-star good!  Italian sausage was 1-poor.  Go to Claro's Italian Market for 5-star freshly made authentic Italian sausages of different flavors--sweet, hot, and on Tuesdays or Wednesdays an additional different flavor like garlic.

My wife had crispy French toast that had corn flakes on it.  They were very thick and came with tons of creamy whipped butter with the option of adding single or multiple dollops of strawberry, raspberry, lemon, or chocolate goo!  The sausage was good!

Overall good food, a large eclectic menu, attentive service, fast turnaround from order to food in front of you, and a nice place, makes this place 4-star Very Good!  I shall return and try the myriad of other unique dishes they have to offer!< /review>

< review>
I wish I could give no stars. I had the gran Toronto burrito my wife had the raspberry crunchy French toast combo and we got the pancake combo for our kids to share. The burrito was supposed to be beans, hash browns sausage eggs and cheese there was 75% beans the hash browns we're not cooked all the way and there were maybe 2 sausage links cut up inside with a canned tomato sauce on top cooked with huge chunks of onions and prices of jalapenos and bell peppers. The French toast was soggy and didn't have enough batter the raspberry sauce was too sweet overpowering the dish and the eggs were undercooked in all dishes, supposed to be scrambled but very runny and the pancakes we're overcooked to an almost rubbery texture. Total fail all around, I don't know why people have rated it so well, maybe they don't have knowledge of what good food should be.< /review>

You can drive right by this place and totally miss it.  It's tucked into an average looking strip mall on the corner of Imperial Hwy and Valley View.

I stopped to get a breakfast burrito at a different place while my car was being serviced.  I saw Amy's and figured I'll just try it.  I'm glad I followed my adventurous streak!

<text>The reviews are right about this person being very amicable, but that does not excuse him of the way he took advantage of my lack of knowledge of how Smog testing works. Because of the high reviews, I went in expecting an honest person who‚Äôd give me honest answers.

My check engine light was on and so I asked him before initiating the test if my vehicle would pass. < rating>
4</rating>
< text>
It's Wendy's. This location usually serves really hot fries so that definitely adds a star but this specific location is kinda run down and a few places in the surrounding area are closed or closing down, lots of homeless in the area. Not that this is Wendy's fault but they could do a little extra to clean up or renovate the location. It's been the same since I was a small child(20+ years) and it's only gotten more destroyed since then.

The staff here is almost always different. Either means a high turnover rate or lots of people doing shorter shifts. This makes for having inconsistencies when ordering food or getting a sauce packet for your food(some people charge you some don't). Also, they have one of those fancy multi-soda dispenser that has the touch screen, that's cool and all but anytime I try to get water it always comes out colored and tasting funny. I tried running the water for awhile to clear out the tubes but still, brown water, residue from sodas and funny taste.

All in all, it's a fast food Wendy's location. Not awful, but not great. Drive-thru is better than going inside because it's so run down. The fries are almost always so hot they burn your mouth, that's a good thing.</text>
